# Case Number: 31E-MM-108062

## Case Summary:
Child Prostitution case against Epstein brought by PBPD, opened 07/25/2006 by FBI Miami Palm Beach RA, resulting in a guilty plea in State Court. This case has remained in Pending Inactive status since 07/25/2017 and case materials have been preserved for a civil litigation hold. The 1B items have been incorporated into the 50D case with new 1B numbers. The remaining 31E-MM file was sent to NY in 2019 in boxes and was housed both in a physical and digital format (DVDs), until we sent it to WFO.

## Notable Details / Clues
- **Classification Markings:** The text frequently begins with "(U//FOUO)". In US government classification, U stands for Unclassified and FOUO stands for For Official Use Only. This indicates these are sensitive government documents likely related to the investigation into Jeffrey Epstein.
- **Jurisdictional Clues:** References to "Legat Canberra" and "Sydney Sub" (likely Sydney Sub-province or similar office) indicate Australian Federal Government involvement, specifically the Department of Justice and/or Attorney-General's office coordinating with US prosecutors (USAO).
- **Specific Entities:** The text explicitly names "Jeffrey Esptein" in the bottom left row. Other references include "Billionaire Investor," "Jailed Tycoon," and "Woman Sues Billionaire Investor."
- **AFP Involved:** The term "AFP" appears multiple times ("REQUEST AFP DELIVER..."), referring to the Australian Federal Police, who were heavily involved in the Epstein case.
- **Repetition:** The line "(U) LEAD SET TO LEGAT CANBERRA COVERED BY THE SYDNEY SUB" appears twice in the visible text, separated by other entries.
- **Victim Support:** The bottom rows detail a protocol for victim notification ("REQUEST HAND DELIVERY OF VICTIM NOTIFICATION"), highlighting a specific administrative process being logged.
- **Redaction Pattern:** The names of victims and potentially the recipients of letters are consistently redacted with black bars, adhering to privacy protocols.
- **Incomplete Sentence Fragments:** Several lines are cut off mid-word or mid-sentence (e.g., "WHEN SHE", "FOR WOR"), suggesting the screenshot captures a larger table that extends beyond the visible frame.
- **Grid Structure:** The right column is essentially empty space with just horizontal dividers, implying it might be reserved for dates, case numbers, or other metadata not fully visible in this crop.

## Detailed Description
The image displays a portion of a formal document, likely a Freedom of Information Act (FOIA) response or a similar government record summary list. The layout consists of a table with horizontal grid lines separating distinct rows. The header "Summary" is visible in bold at the top left.

The document lists various data holdings and information requests regarding a specific entity (whose name is heavily redacted). The entries are categorized by source agency or database.
-   **Top Section:** The first five rows list telecommunications providers. These include "(U) T-Mobile USA, Inc", "(U) At&" (likely AT&T), "(U) Bell South", and "(U) Metro PCS". Beside these names, the text reads "Subscriber Information" or "Subscriber and Toll Information".
-   **Middle Section:** Following the telecom entries is an entry for the "(U) Palm Beach County Health Department - Certificate of Birth fo...", which trails off into a heavy redaction block.
-   **Bulk List:** The majority of the document (rows 7 through roughly row 30) consists of repetitive entries indicating the existence of records on a subject. These entries predominantly start with "(U) Biographical file" or "(U) Biographical files".
-   **Redactions:** Almost every row contains significant portions covered by solid black bars. In some rows (like row 7), smaller bars cover specific fields like "dob" (date of birth). Other rows feature long, continuous black bars obscuring names and other personal identifiers on the right side of the page.
-   **Footer:** At the very bottom right corner, outside the table grid, is a unique identifier code: "EFTA02730917".

    -   "(U) Biographical file, MySpace information, and original notes fo"

-   **Bottom Right ID:** EFTA02730917

## Notable Details / Clues
-   **Classification Markings:** The text "(U)" preceding most entries is standard for U.S. federal documents, indicating the record is "Unrated" or "Unclassified."
-   **Historical Context:** The inclusion of "MySpace information" in many rows suggests these records pertain to an era where MySpace was a primary social media platform (roughly 2005–2010).
-   **Data Privacy Implications:** The extensive redaction covers what are almost certainly protected identifiers like names, Social Security Numbers (implied by "Biographical file"), and dates of birth.
-   **Document Type:** This looks like a spreadsheet export or a printed table from a database used to catalog requests for records on a specific individual.
-   **Geographic Specificity:** The mention of "Palm Beach County Health Department" places the jurisdictional origin of at least one record in Florida.
-   **Redaction Strategy:** The use of long black bars suggests a policy of obscuring the subject's identity to protect privacy while releasing the document for other purposes (like showing the *types* of records held without revealing the specific person).
-   **Agency Types:** The mix of telecom companies, health departments, and social media platforms (MySpace) highlights a comprehensive data mining approach often seen in intelligence or law enforcement investigations.

90A-NY-3151227

On 02/28/2025, FBI-NYO opened case 90A-NY-3151227, a death investigation case on 08/12/2019 after JEFFERY EPSTEIN was discovered unresponsive in his jail cell at MCC on 08/10/2019. Two Correctional Officers were indicted for false records and conspiracy and subsequently self-surrendered to the FBI on 11/19/2019. In May 2021, SDNY entered a deferred prosecution agreement with the two Correctional Officers for a period of 6 months and the terms were satisfied. 90C-NY-3154599 is a contraband at MCC case in which EPSTEIN is referenced. 9A-NY-3144791 is a threat to victim case in which EPSTEIN is referenced.
